üî∞Convert FAT - NTFSüî∞

To convert a FAT partition to NTFS, perform the following steps.

1) Open 'Command Prompt'.

2) At the command prompt, type the following-

CONVERT [driveletter]: /FS:NTFS.

'Convert.exe' will attempt to convert the partition to NTFS.

NOTE :- Although the chance of corruption or data loss during the conversion from FAT to NTFS is minimal, it is best to perform a full backup of the data on the drive that it is to be converted prior to executing the convert command.

We have discussed all type of html list in previous posts. Now, we will discuss about various Html tags one by one in alphabetical orders (a-z).

Today we are going to discuss about <acronym> tag and <abbr> tag. <abbr> tag represents abbreviations.

What is acronym or abbreviations?
Acronym/abbreviations are formed by using the first letter of each word.

For example - Suppose we have a phrase which is World Health organization .
So the acronym or abbreviations of World Health organization is "WHO".

We will see an example of <abbr> tag because acronym tag has been deprecated from HTML5. Both <abbr> and <acronym> tag is same as I said above.

What is the use of <abbr> tag?
<abbr> tag and "title" attribute is used to give the full text information of an abbreviations.

Syntax =
<abbr title="World Health organization"> WHO
</abbr>

An Html code of <abbr> tag :-
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
<title> Abbreviations </title>
</head>
<body><abbr title="National Aeronautics and Space Administration">NASA</abbr>
</body>
</html>

Whenever You move the pointer or mouse cursor to NASA word. It will show the full abbreviation of that word.

Extra information :-
<acronym> tag was used in previous html versions. It works same as <abbr> tag. #Don't_use_acronym_tag.

Syntax -
<acronym title="Full text information of an abbreviation word">
Here you should write an abbreviation word.
</acronym>

Example -
<acronym title="National Aeronautics and Space Administration">NASA</acronym>

Hello Guys, I hope you are enjoying my post and learning something new from each post.

Today, we are going to discuss about <article> tag. Let's start :

What is the use of <article> tag?

The <article> tag was introduced in html5. It is used to define an independent and self contained content in our html document. In simple word, we can say it is used to define an article.

What type of content you can include in <article> tag?

You can include a Blog Post, Forum Post, Magazines, News etc.

#Remember_this - You can use multiple <article> tag in a single html document.

Now let's see syntax and an example of <article> tag.

Syntax -

<article>
Here you will write your Content of an article like a Blog Post, magazines, News etc.
</article>

An exampe of <article> tag -

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
<title>Article tag</title>
</head>
<body>
<h2>Topic name of Article</h2>
<article>
Here you will write your Content of an article like a Blog Post, magazines, News etc.
</article>
</body>
</html>

Thank you guys!

¬´system32¬ª)

well,there is a great way of hacking an administrator account from a guest account by

Concept

Press shift key 5 times and the sticky key dialog shows up.This works even at the
logon screen. But If we replace the sethc.exe which is responsible for the sticky key
dialog,with cmd.exe, and then call sethc.exe by pressing shift key 5 times at logon
screen,we will get a command prompt with administrator privilages because no user
has logged on. From there we can hack the administrator password,even from a guest
account.

Prerequisites
Guest account with write access to system 32.

When asked to overwrite, overwrite the sethc.exe.

Now Log out from your guest account and at the user select window,press shift key
5 times.
Instead of Sticky Key confirmation dialog,command prompt with full administrator
privileges will open.
Press shift key 5 times and command prompt will open.

you like and press enter.
You will see ‚Äú The Command completed successfully‚Äù and then exit the command
prompt and login into administrator with your new password.
Congrats You have hacked admin from guest account.

Ephemeral /ADD‚Äù where ‚ÄúEphemeral‚Äù is the username you would like to add with
administrator privileges. Then hide your newly created admin account by -

Go to registry editor and navigate to this key
[HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Windows
NT\CurrentVersion\Winlogon\SpecialAccounts\UserList]

Here create a new DWORD value, write its name as the ‚Äúuser name‚Äù that u created
for your admin account and live with your admin account forever

Now We are going to learn about <aside> tag. Let's start-

What is the use of <aside> tag?

The <aside> tag is used to define those content that is indirectly related to the original content of an html document. It was introduced in html5.

Syntax of <aside> tag -
<aside>
Here You will write the related content.
</aside>

An Example to show How can we use <aside> tag in our html document -

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
<title> Aside Tag </title>
</head>
<body>
I visited Taj Mahal
<aside>
The Taj Mahal is one of the most beautiful monuments in India.
</aside>
</body>
</html>

Hii everybody,

Today we start our latest and pure ethical hacking course.

Our first topic is about 'Footprinting'
21:23
What is Footprinting?

Footprinting¬†(also known as reconnaissance) is the technique used for gathering information about computer systems and the entities they belong to. To get this information, a hacker might use various tools and technologies. This information is very useful to a hacker who is trying to crack a whole system.
21:23
How Footprinting perform?

With the help of a tool named 'whois'.

This tool is already installed in Kali Linux and in android u have to install it in Termux.
21:23
How whois works?

WHOIS is a web application used to get information about the target website, such as the administrator's e-mail address and details about the registration. WHOIS is a very large database and contains information of approximately all the websites. It can be searched by domain name

Other methods of Footprinting?

By using search engines like Google.
21:23
Information to be gathered using Footprinting--

If the attack is to be performed on a company, then the following information will be gathered.

Company details,employee details and their email addressses.

Relation with other companies.

Project details involving other companies.

Legal documents of the company.

News relating company website.

Patents and Trademarks regarding that particular company.

Important dates regarding new projects
21:23
FootPrinting_Tutorial.webm
Not included, change data exporting settings to download.
3.5 MB
FOOTPRINTING TUTORIAL
21:23
Hii everybody our next topic is 'Network Scanning'.

So let's start our topic-
21:23
What is Scanning?

Scanning is a set of procedures for identifying live hosts, ports, and services, discovering Operating system and architecture of target system, Identifying vulnerabilities and threats in the network. Network scanning is used to create a profile of the target organization.

Scanning refers to collecting more information using complex and aggressive reconnaissance techniques.
21:23
Scanning Methodology--

Check for Live Systems:¬†Ping scan checks for the live system by sending ICMP echo request packets. If a system is alive, the system responds with ICMP echo reply packet containing details of TTL, packet size etc.¬†

Check for Open Ports:¬†Port scanning helps us to find out open ports, services running on them, their versions etc. Nmap is the powerful tool used mainly for this purpose.

We have various types of scan:

Connect scan:¬†Identifies open ports by establishing a TCP handshake with the target.¬†

Nmap command:¬†nmap -sT -v -p- <TargetIP>

Half-open scan¬†otherwise known as Stealth scan used to scan the target in a stealthy way by not completing the TCP handshake by abruptly resetting the communication.



Nmap command: nmap -sS -v <TargetIp>

XMAS scan:¬†This is also called as inverse TCP scanning. This works by sending packets set with PSH, URG, FIN flags. The targets do not respond if the ports are open and send a reset response if ports are closed.


FIN scan:¬†Fin flag is set in the TCP packets sent to the target. open ports doe does not respond while closed ports send a reset response.


Nmap command: nmap -SF <targetIp>

ACK scan:¬†Here the attacker sets the ACK flag in the TCP header and the target's port status is gathered based on window size and TTL value of RESET packets received from the target.¬†

Nmap command: nmap -SA -v <targetip>

Null Scan:¬†Works by sending TCP packets with no flags set to the target. Open ports do not respond while closed ports respond with a RESET packet.


Nmap Command: ¬†nmap -sN -p- <targetIP>

Idle Scan:¬†Here the attacker tries to mask his identity uses an idle machine on the network to probe the status details of target ports.


Nmap command : nmap -Pn -sI ZombieIp TargetIp

Banner Grabbing

Banner grabbing is a process of collecting information like operating system details, the name of the service running with its version number etc.

Vulnerability scanning:

Mainly automated tools are used for this purpose. These automated scanners scan the target to find out vulnerabilities or weakness in the target organization which can be exploited by the attackers. Vulnerabilities include application vulnerabilities, configuration vulnerabilities, network vulnerabilities, operating system vulnerabilities etc.

Some examples include operating system is not updated, default passwords used, plain text protocols used, vulnerable protocols running etc.

Tools: Nessus, Acunetix

Draw Network Diagrams

With the information gathered, the attacker can come up with a network diagram which might give him information about network and architecture of the target organization helping him to identify the target easily¬†

Tools: Network View, Opmanager etc

Prepare Proxies

Proxies can use to maintain the anonymity of the attacker by masking the IP address. It can capture information passing through it since it acts as an intermediary between client and server and the attacker can access the resources remotely using the proxies.¬†

Eg: TOR browsers, Onion sites etc, Proxify, Psiphon etc

Countermeasures:¬†

Configure IDS and firewall to block probes.

Keep firewall, routers, IDS firmware update

Run port scanners to verify the security of the target.

Add rules in firewall restricting access to ports.

Disable ICMP based scanning at firewall.

@costlessknowledge
Today we are going to discuss about <audio> tag.

<audio> tag Details -

It is used to insert an audio in our Webpages. Currently, <audio> tag supports three format of audios such as MP3, WAV, OGG.

Let's see syntax of <audio> tag in various formats -

1. <audio src="url" type="audio/mpeg">
</audio>

2. <audio src="url" type="audio/wav">
</audio>

3. <audio src="url" type="audio/ogg">
</audio>

Points to be Remember -
1. If Your html document & audio in same folder, You can simply use the file_name.mp3 .

2. if your html document on desktop or any folder and audio file kept at different location, You need to give the absolute Url of audio file in "src" attributes.
07:24
In previous post, I have told you about <audio> tag and how to use this tag in our html document?

In this post, I am going to tell you about the Various Attributes of <audio> tag. So let's start -

1. Controls - It will add the Play, Pause and Volume Button in our html webpage.

Syntax - <audio src="url" controls>
</audio>

2. src - It specifies the location of audio file. We have already discussed in Previous post.

3. Loop - It is used to play the inserted audio again and again.

Syntax - <audio src="url" controls loop>
</audio>

4. autoplay - It is used to play the music automatically when the page loads.

Syntax -
<audio src="url" controls autoplay>
</audio>

5. muted - It is used to mute the audio
.
Syntax - <audio src="url" controls muted>
</audio>

6. Preload - It is used to specifies that how do you want to load the audio file, When the Page loads.

Note - it won't work if you have used #autoplay attributes.

#preload attributes contain three types of Value -
1. auto - It is used to load the entire audio file When the page loads.

Syntax -
<audio src="url" controls preload="auto">
</audio>

2. None - It is used to tell the browser that audio file should not be loaded when the page loads.

Syntax -
<audio src="url" controls preload="none">
</audio>

3. metadata - It is used to load the metadata When the page loads.

Syntax -
<audio src="url" controls preload="metadata">
</audio>

#Points_to_be_Remember -
Controls attribute must we used , while inserting an audio file in our webpage otherwise You won't get the Control button such as play, pause, volume.

If You have any Query ask from me @Knowledge_About_Everything

Today We are going to discuss about <b> tag.

Why we use <b> tag?
It is used to define a #bold text.

Syntax -
<b> Anuj </b>

An example to show how can we implement<b> tag in an Html document?

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
<title> Bold text </title>
</head>
<body>
<b>
Name - Anuj Kumar
</b>
</body>
</html>
13:22
In this post we are going to use <base> tag.
So let's start -

Why do we use <base> tag?
It is used to define the base URL and base target for all relative URLs in an html document.. We can use a maximum of one <base> tag in an html document and it must be written inside the <head> tag. It doesn't have closing tag and does not support any Event attributes.

Let's talk about Various Attributes of <base> tag -

1. href - It is used to define the base Url of all relatives URL in an html document.

Syntax -
<base href="URL">

2. target - It is used to define the default target for all hyperlinks and forms in the page.

Syntax -
<base target="Different Value">

Now let's see Various Values of target attribute -
üëâ _blank - It is used to opens the link in a new tab.
Syntax -
<base href="URL" target="_blank">


üëâ _self - It is used to opens the link in a same frame or in a same tab. It is default.
Syntax -
<base target="_self">

üëâ _parent - It is used to opens the link in the parent frame. If there is no parent, this option behaves the same way as¬†_self.
Syntax -
<base target="_parent">

üëâ _top - It is used to opens the link in the full body of window. If there is no parent, this option behaves the same way as¬†_self.
Syntax -
<base target="_top">

üëâ framename - It is used to opens the link in a named frame. For using this Value we have to define the name of a frame. For example - I have defined a frame name is Anuj, In this case Syntax should be -

<base target="Anuj">

Note - You can use both attributes together in <base> tag.
Syntax -
<base href="URL" target="_blank">

In this post we are going to discuss about <bdo> tag.
Let's start -

Why do we use <bdo> tag?
Bdo stands for Bi-directional Override and
It is used to override the text direction. It can be Right to left or Left to right.

Let's talk about Attributes of <bdo> tag -
This tag contains only One attribute which is "dir" attribute. dir attribute specifies the text direction of the text inside a <bdo> element.

"dir" attribute supports two values -
1. rtl - It is used to define the text direction from right to left.
Syntax -
<bdo dir="rtl"> Write Text Here </bdo>

2. ltr - It is used to define the text direction from left to right. It is default.
Syntax -
<bdo dir="ltr"> Write Text Here </bdo>

I am giving An Example Code of Right to left direction -

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
<title> BDO tag </title>
</head>
<body>
<bdo dir="rtl">
Name - Anuj Kumar
</bdo>
</body>
</html>

We are going to discuss about <blockquote> tag in this post.
Let's start -

Why do we use <blockquote> tag?
Ans. - It is used to define a section that is quoted from another source. It contains only One attribute.

Attribute Name -
Cite - It specifies the main source of Quotation. It doesn't display anything in the browser but it can be used by search engines.

Syntax -
<blockquote cite="url"> Your content Here </blockquote>
You can use Relative and absolute Url.

An example code -
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
<title> Blockquote tag </title>
</head>
<body>
<b>Taj Mahal</b>
<blockquote cite="https://www.tajmahal.gov.in">
One knows that ‚ÄòThe Taj‚Äô is one amongst the World‚Äôs Wonders!
One knows that it is one amongst the UNESCO World Heritage Sites!!
One knows The Taj as a legend of eternal love of an Emperor for his favourite Queen!!!
</blockquote>
</body>
</html>

Today, we are going to discuss about <cite> tag. Let's start -

Why do we use <cite> tag?
It is used to define the title of a work. Work can be a tweet, facebook post, blog post, studying etc. It will display the Work title in italic form.

Syntax -
<cite>Write work title here</cite>

An Example code -
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
<title>Cite tag</title>
</head>
<body>
I have done a <cite>Tweet</cite>
</body>
</html>

1080x855, 38.2 KB
Now, We are going to discuss about <code> tag.
Let's start -

Why do we use <code> tag?
It is used to define a piece of computer code. By default, The content inside the <code> element is displayed in monospace font.

Syntax -
<code> Computer code or functions Here </code>

An example code -
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
<title>Code Tag</title>
</head>
<body>
<code>getchar()</code> is used to get or read the input (i.e a single character) at runtime.
</body>
</html>

üî∞What Is Net Phishing?üî∞

Phishing is the attempt to acquire sensitive information such as usernames, passwords, and credit card details (and some indirectly, money) by masquerading as a trustworthy entity in an electronic communication.

This method has been used since ages and is still filling most¬†of our mailboxes with scam mail from banks, lottery and viagra¬†offers. When performing a net phishing attack, the goal is to¬†throw a bate to as many people as possible and make them¬†arrive to an authority site (such as a bank or e.g. Facebook)¬†which is identical or similar to the original.

The victim is then asked for credentials. This credentials can¬†then be used to take over a account and e.g. transfer money¬†to a foreign country.

üí•How to Check your IP information

You might need your PC's IP address if you want to set up an Internet connection, allow other people to connect to your PC, or need to troubleshoot network problems.

Follow the Steps: (Without Using CMD)

Step 1:
In Windows 8.1, select the Start button , start typing View network connections, and then select it in the list.

In Windows 7, open Network Connections by selecting the Start button Start button icon and then selecting Control Panel. In the search box, type adapter, and then, under Network and Sharing Center, select View network connections.

Step 2: Select an active network connection, and then, in the toolbar, select View status of this connection. (You might need to select the chevron icon to find this command.)

Step 3: Select Details.

Step 4: Your PC's IP address appears in the Value column, next to IPv4 Address.


Follow the Steps : (Using the CMD)

Step 1: Open Run Dialog Box (Press Win+R)

Step 2: Type CMD and hit Enter

Step 3: Type ipconfig and hit Enter

Step 4: Look for Default Gateway under your network adapter for your Router's IP address.
Look for IPv4 Address under the same adapter section to find your computer's IP address.
If you use a virtual private network for your business, its connection will have its own section and list your proxy IP address under IPv4 Address.

üî∞ Types of hacking üî∞

üëÅ‚Äçüó®When we execute an ethical hacking is necessary to establish its scope to develop a
realistic schedule of work and to deliver the economic proposal to the client. To determine
the project extent we need to know at least three basic elements: the type of hacking that
we will conduct, the modality and the additional services that customers would like to
include with the contracted service.

‚¨õÔ∏èDepending on where we execute the penetration testing, an ethical hacking can be
external or internal.‚¨õÔ∏è

‚ñ´Ô∏èExternal pentesting ‚ñ´Ô∏è

ü¶†This type of hacking is done from the Internet against the client‚Äôs public network
infrastructure; that is, on those computers in the organization that are exposed to the
Internet because they provide a public service. Example of public hosts: router, firewall,
web server, mail server, name server, etc.‚ú®

‚ñ´Ô∏èInternal pentesting ‚ñ´Ô∏è

ü¶†As the name suggests, this type of hacking is executed from the customer‚Äôs
internal network, from the point of view of a company employee, consultant, or business
associate that has access to the corporate network.
In this type of penetration test we often find more security holes than its external
counterpart, because many system administrators are concerned about protecting the
network perimeter and underestimate the internal attackers. The latter is a mistake, since
studies show that the majority of successful attacks come from inside the company. To cite
an example, in a survey conducted on computer security to a group of businessmen in the
UK, when they were asked ‚Äúwho the attackers are‚Äù, these figures were obtained: 25%
external, 75% internal‚ú®

‚ñ´Ô∏èHacking modalities ‚ñ´Ô∏è

ü¶† Depending on the information that the customer provides to the consultant, an
ethical hacking service could be executed in one of three modes: black-box, gray-box or
white-box. The method chosen will affect the cost and duration of the penetration testing
audit, since the lesser the information received, the greater the time in research invested by
the auditor. ‚ú®

‚ñ´Ô∏èBlack box hacking ‚ñ´Ô∏è

ü¶† This mode is applicable to external testing only. It is called so because the client
only gives the name of the company to the consultant, so the auditor starts with no
information, the infrastructure of the organization is a ‚Äúblack box‚Äù.
While this type of audit is considered more realistic, since the external attacker
who chooses an X victim has no further information to start that the name of the
organization that is going to attack, it is also true that it requires a greater investment of
time and therefore the cost incurred is higher too. Additionally, it should be noted that the
ethical hacker - unlike the cracker - does not have all the time in the world to perform
penetration testing, so the preliminary analysis cannot extend beyond what is possible in
practical terms because of cost/time/benefit. ‚ú®

‚ñ´Ô∏èGray box hacking ‚ñ´Ô∏è

ü¶† This method is often used synonymously to refer to internal pentestings.
Nevertheless, some auditors also called gray-box-hacking an external test in which the
client provides limited information on public computers to be audited. Example: a list of
data such as IP address and type/function of the equipment (router, web-server, firewall,
etc.). When the term is applied to internal testing, it is given that name because the
consultant receives the same access that an employee would have like having his laptop
connected to the internal network and the NIC configured properly (IP address, subnet
mask, gateway and DNS server); but does not obtain additional information such as:
username/password to join a domain, the existence of related subnets, etc. ‚ú®

Today we are going to discuss about <dialog> tag.

What is the use of <dialog> tag?
It is used to define a dialog box. It is very easy to create a pop-up dialog box by using dialog tag.

Note - This tag is not supported in Internet Explorer.

Syntax -
<dialog> Dialog box content </dialog>

<dialog> tag contains One Attribute.
1. Open - It is used to define that dialog box is active and user can interact with it.
When the open attribute is not set, the dialog won't be shown to the user.

Syntax -
<dialog open> Dialog box content
</dialog>

An example code -
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
<title>Dialog Box </title>
</head>
<body>
<dialog open> I am a dialog box</dialog>
</body>
</html>
17:09
In this post we are going to discuss about <dfn> tag.

What is the use of <dfn> tag?
It is used to define the instance of a term in an html document. By default, The term inside the <dfn> tag will display in italic.

Syntax -
<dfn> Term name Here </dfn>

An example code -
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
<title>Dfn Tag</title>
</head>
<body>
<dfn>Taj Mahal</dfn> is so special because of its enormous beauty.
</body>
</html>

From Tomorrow we are going to learn about Table and see How can we make table in html.

How to shut down your computer through C Program.

To shutdown your computer using C program, You'll need to call the¬†system()¬†function which will call the¬†cmd.
stdlib.h contain the system() function and it is used to run any executable file.

C Program Code - 

#include<stdio.h>
#include<conio.h>
 #include<stdlib.h> 
void main() 
{  
char c;  
printf("Do you want to shutdown your PC/Computer (y/n) : ");  
scanf("%c",&c);  
if(c=='y' || c=='Y')
system("C:\\Windows\\System32\\shutdown /s /t 0"); 
else
printf("You don't wanna shut down your PC/Computer");
getch();
}


Note - Save the file with .c extension.
/s represents shutdown
/t represents Time means after how much time you wanna shut down your pc. If you will not define the time, By default it will shut down your pc after 30sec.

‚¨õÔ∏èHow to Install a Complete Linux Distro on Android‚¨õÔ∏è

‚ñ´Ô∏èFor users who want to experience a complete desktop OS on their Android phone, especially tech-savvy people who don‚Äôt want to carry around a laptop or tablet, it‚Äôs entirely possible to install a fully-functional Linux OS on your Android phone.
You will need a rooted phone for this operation ‚Äì you can search Appuals for a root guide for your device if you aren‚Äôt already rooted. Once you‚Äôre rooted though, the process is fairly simple.‚ñ´Ô∏è

Requirements
BusyBox
VNC Viewer
Linux Deploy

ü¶†The first thing you‚Äôll want to do is install BusyBox ‚Äì either directly from Google Play store, or the Magisk BusyBox module if you‚Äôre rooted with MagiskSU.

If you install BusyBox from the Google Play store, you just need to download the app, launch it, and hit the ‚ÄúInstall‚Äù button from inside the app.

ü¶†If you‚Äôre rooted with MagiskSU, you need to launch Magisk Manager and go to Settings, then enable the ‚ÄúEnable Busybox‚Äù button, which will utilize Magisk‚Äôs built-in BusyBox for your device.
What BusyBox does is allow your Android system to use Linux commands normally not accessible to you ‚Äì many root apps depend on this. With BusyBox installed, you‚Äôre now going to launch Linux Deploy on your device.

ü¶†In the Linux Deploy menu, choose ‚ÄúDownload‚Äù, and then you‚Äôll be presented with an options menu. Here is where you‚Äôll configure your Linux distro before it‚Äôs installed, and I‚Äôll explain the important settings:

ü¶†Distribution ‚Äì Choose your Linux distro to install. There‚Äôs quite a large list, but the most user-friendly would be Ubuntu.
Distribution suite ‚Äì Choose a version of the Linux distro you selected above.
Architecture ‚Äì Do not change this, it is automatically selected based on your device.
Image size (MB) ‚Äì The default is 512, but you should change this to a higher available number. Just don‚Äôt enter a number greater than 4095mb.
SSH Settings ‚Äì You‚Äôll need to change the default port of 22 here, but Android devices can only use ports about 1024. Most users would opt for port 2222.
Custom mounts ‚Äì If you want to access your Android filesystem from within the Linux distro, go to ‚ÄúMount points‚Äù and choose the ones you need. If you cannot enable the internal storage, change the default storage mount /storage/emulated/0 to /data/media/0.

ü¶†You should set your username to ‚Äúroot‚Äù ‚Äì this will give you permanent super-user access inside the Linux distro. When everything has been configured, press the Install button, and after it‚Äôs finished, you may launch the Linux distro with the Start button ‚Äì but this will launch it in chroot, which is like a command-line terminal. So we need to access the GUI using the VNC Viewer tool.

ü¶†Launch VNC and set the address to ‚Äúlocalhost:5900‚Äù and enter your password. You now have a fully-functioning Linux desktop OS on your Android phone. You may want to begin installing Linux apps, which is done through the Linux terminal. Here are a few worth grabbing (use the commands in the terminal):
LibreOffice ‚Äì apt-get install libreoffice
Firefox ‚Äì apt-get install iceweasel
Python Idle ‚Äì apt-get install idle
GIMP ‚Äì apt-get install gimp
DropBox ‚Äì apt-get install nautilus-dropbox

Today we are going to discuss about attributes of <table> tag. All these attributes has been deprecated from html5 and we don't use these attributes.

Attributes are as follow -
üëâ align - It is used to align the table. It contain three values.

1. left - It is used to align the table in left. (Default)

Syntax -
<table align="left">


2. right - It is used to align the table in right.

Syntax -
<table align="right">


3. center - It is used to align the table in center.

Syntax -
<table align="center">

_____________________________________
üëâ border - It is used to define the border around the table cells.. if we give the border value to 0 then No border will be displayed around the table cells.


Syntax - 

<table border="0"> ( For No border)

<table border="1">   (For border)

_____________________________________
üëâ width - It is used to define the width of table. We can give the value of width in two types in pixels or in percent. 

Syntax - 
<table width="100"> (Pixel syntax)
<table width="100%"> (Percent syntax)

_____________________________________
üëâ bgcolor - It is used to define the background color of table. We can give the value of bgcolor in three ways -

1. by color name
2. By hex code
3. By rgb code 

Syntax - 
1. <table bgcolor="Red">
2. <table bgcolor="#000000">
3. <table bgcolor="rgb(255,255,255)">

_____________________________________

21:01
Today one of our member asked from me What is the difference between <stdio.h> and "stdio.h"

Let's see what is <stdio.h> and What is the work ?
<stdio.h> is a header file which is available in "include" directory of the system. When we write #include<stdio.h> preprocessor search directly in "include" directory and it won't search outside of this directory.

Let's see what is the "stdio.h" and it's work?
"stdio.h" also works same as <stdio.h> but it has an advantage that it will look the file stdio.h in the current directory as well as the specified list of directories as mentioned in the #include search path.

As you all know your stdio.h file available in the "include" directory or folder. and when you remove the stdio.h file from "include" directory then it won't work. But when you are using "stdio.h" you can simply give the full path of stdio.h file where you have kept the file. And it will work because it will search stdio.h file in given path and will search in the current directory as well. Where by default stdio.h file is available.

Let's assume we have kept the stdio.h file in the Turboc3 folder then our path will be like this C:\TURBOC3\stdio.h

Syntax for <stdio.h> - 
#include<stdio.h>


(It will give the error after checking the file in "include" directory.)

Syntax for "stdio.h" - 

#include "stdio.h"

(if we will write in this way it will also give us an error. But there is one more way , we can give the full path of stdio.h file. )

#include "C:\TURBOC3\stdio.h"

Now this will work fine ‚úåÔ∏èbecause now it will check the given path as well.



Note -
#include<C:\TURBOC3\stdio.h> it will also work with angular brackets when we write in this way. But As a Programmer we never use this. #include<stdio.h> can only be used to check the stdio.h file in the "include" directory.

I hope you have understand all the basic difference. Thank You guys. If any Query Msg me at @Knowledge_About_Everything‚úåÔ∏è

‚Äç ‚Äã‚ÄãWhat will machine learning look like in 20 years?

1. We are still far away from AGI
Current generation machine learning systems are still very far away from something that could legitimately be called artificial ‚Äúintelligence‚Äù. The systems we have right now are phenomenal at pattern recognition, but it is very far away from an intelligent system.

2. Traditional programming is not going away
Machine Learning excels where dealing with the messiness of the real world, lots of data is available and no reasonably fundamental model is available. If any of these are not true, you generally don‚Äôt have to settle for a machine learning model - the traditional alternatives are superior.

3. Machine Learning will augment most traditional tasks
Anytime one of the traditional systems needs to interact with a human, there is an opportunity for machine-learning based augmentation. For example, a programmer looking at error messages, could use a machine learning system that looks at the error messages and suggests a course of action. In addition, machine learning systems can learn from massive amounts of data very rapidly and on a global scale.

4. We‚Äôll get better at learning from small or noisy data
At the moment machine learning systems mostly require large amounts of relatively clean, curated, data sets.

5. We‚Äôll see ML systems be combined with traditional approaches
We are very excited about physics-based ML approaches where you combine a neural network with knowledge of an underlying physical model in order to outperform both pure ML approaches and approaches relying solely on the physical process.
23:00
‚Äç ‚Äã‚ÄãSmart cities are an AI-powered dystopia that‚Äôs already happening

What are the prospects and implications of AI recognition in the smart cities of the future?

Consumer-based recognition as it stands
We‚Äôre already seeing it in the ability to buy things on your iPhone or online and authorize a purchase via facial recognition. I think biometrics is probably the next step ‚Äì companies are pioneering a lot of work around the ability to generate and invoke purchases via voice recognition.

AI recognition‚Äôs association with privacy concerns
To make full use of the security provided by AI recognition technology, integration is likely to be comprehensively interspersed across the smart cities of the future. At present, using such tech is more of a conscious choice ‚Äì holding your phone up to your face to unlock it, for example. The notion of widespread cameras and sensors, especially throughout metropolitan areas, might be met with the same uncertainty as an overabundance of security cameras.

Citizen tracking and targeting
The implications of a person‚Äôs exposure to constant identification aren‚Äôt restricted to the state‚Äôs use of the technology. At a consumer level, there is the potential for users to open themselves up to entirely new levels of targeted advertising through retailers‚Äô use of AI identification in stores.

The current state of AI development
Development for development‚Äôs sake could pose a real problem as AI makes the transition from the casual consumer tech of the present into the essential infrastructural tech of the future. Public trust needs to be there, but so does the public‚Äôs recognition that these AI solutions actually solve a specific problem.

Creating a transparent system
This concept of accountability will most likely be a crucial condition in the public willingness to accept AI recognition as an ingrained part of future cities. As mentioned previously, the potential applications for the technology are many, but these applications must be developed through a framework of problem-solving.

We have used two functions -
üëâ
initwindow()

üëâ
readimagefile()


Let's see definitions of these two functions -

üëâ
initwindow()

function is available in the winbgim implementation of BGI graphics. We don't need to include conio.h; just include graphics.h, it will work. it is used to define the graphics window size and title. By default, graphic window name is "Windows BGI"

Basic syntax - initwindow(width, height, "title");


üëâ
readimagefile()

function reads a BMP, GIF, JPG, ICO, EMF or WMF image file and displays in the graphics window. It is available in the winbgim implementation of BGI graphics.

Basic syntax -
readimagefile("imageFilename" , left, top, right, bottom);

We are going to discuss about _setcursortype() functions in C language.

What is _setcursortype() function ?

This function is used to define the cursor type means which type of cursor should be displayed on the output screen. This function contained by conio.h header file.

We can use three types of values ‚úåÔ∏è
üëâ_NOCURSOR - It is used to define that no cursor should be displayed.

Syntax - _setcursortype(_NOCURSOR);

üëâ_SOLIDCURSOR - It is used to define that solid block cursor should be displayed.

Syntax -
_setcursortype(_SOLIDCURSOR);

üëâ_NORMALCURSOR - It is used to define an underscore cursor which is by default displayed on the screen.

Syntax -
_setcursortype(_NORMALCURSOR);

Note - Don't use this function in Win32 GUI applications.

Difference Between Dark Web And Deep Web
This is the major confusion between the majority of us- Interpreting that the dark web and deep web same. Both these deep and dark web are completely different though there existence a similarity that we can‚Äôt google it any info from both of them.

The Web is divided into 3 layers:
The Surface Web
The Deep Web
Dark Web
1. The Surface Web: It‚Äôs the most common Internet everyone uses to the read articles, news , shop gadgets‚Ä¶etc. Just consider that this is the ‚Äúregular‚Äù Internet.* like Google, Twitter, YouTube and so on. If we want to find more information we search them which leads us to the different website which is on the surface web i.e indexed page and visible to the search engines.

FOR ACCESSING Surface Web

Just search something in any search engine either google or yahoo or nay other platform, so this is a surface web , even google is a part of the surface web.

2. The Deep Web: The deep web is a subset of the Internet which isn‚Äôt indexed by the major search engines. This means that you have to visit on those places directly instead of being able to search for them on internet or search engine. So there aren‚Äôt directions or any way to get there, but they‚Äôre waiting if you have an address. The Deep Web is largely there simply because of the Internet is too large for search engines to cover it completely. So the Deep Web is the long tail of what‚Äôs left out, like someone‚Äôs company database (as only specific people can able to access it or only some need these)[not to be confused for the intranet , its another thing].

FOR ACCESSING The Deep Web

You will require the exact address or URL of these pages because they are not indexed and can‚Äôt be searched with your search engine.

3. The Dark Web : Now this is something that have majority of people are unaware of it (also called Darknet) ‚Äì a subset of the Deep Web that is not only not indexed, but that can also requires something special to be able to access it, ex. specific proxying ( like TOR ) software or authentication to gain access of these types of websites. These pages also requires additional sub-network like Freenet, I2P, TOR. These and it is often associated with the criminal activity at various degrees, it also including buying and selling drugs, gambling, etc. Have you heard about SILK ROAD , it was started in .onion sites only.

DARK WEB

The dark Web is comprised of different types of websites that are visible to the public, but their IP address details are intentionally hidden for the public and others. These websites can be visited by anyone through internet, but it is not easy to find their server details on which their corresponding site is running, and it is difficult to track their one hosting the site.

The dark Web concept is achievable with the help of different types of anonymity tools available on internet. Some of the popular tools are Tor and I2P. The dark Web is popular for both the black market and user protections, so it has both the positive and negative aspects.

This Web ensures that one‚Äôs privacy by effectively hiding the server and their IP details from the public. The dark Web also requires special kinds of software to access it. This software acts as a gateway to the dark Websites. Once the user gains access to these websites, then all the dark websites and other services can be accessed in the simple way with help of their own browsers.

The dark Web also includes a wide range of the networks, from small, friend-to-friend/peer-to-peer networks to the large, popular networks such as Freenet, I2P and Tor, operated by public organizations and individuals to access the dark web. Some of the categories are Web-based hidden services that include:

Drugs

Fraud

Gambling

Chatting

Hacking

Hosting

Search

Anonymity

Whistle blower

Most dark websites are not directly accessible via the normal search made through a search engine like google and yahoo; they are effectively hide themselves. They are accessible only if their addresses of those sites are known to the user. Some of the methods which hide websites from the normal searches are:

Private Web which requires your registration

Contextual Web varies as per IP address

Limited access to the content where access is limited to certain licensed contents

Scripted content which is accessible only through links that is generated by JavaScript or dynamically downloaded from the Web servers.

Non-HTML/textual content

Softwares where the data are intentionally hidden from the regular Internet users and made it accessible only with special types of softwares, such as Tor, I2P, or by the other‚Äôs darknet software‚Äôs.

Web archives which are archived versions of the Web pages, including the websites which have become inaccessible, and are not indexed by the search engines such as Google or Yahoo.

The industries which operate over the dark Web are also known as darknet markets; this also includes black market sales of illegal products, to stay hidden from the governments and law of enforcement agencies. The dark Web is also used in other ways, just ike communication between whistleblowers and protecting users from attacks or from the surveillance to ensure privacy in the communication. But the dark Web is mostly used in the black markets as it promises total anonymity.

How to Hack WiFi passwords [Using Kali Linux]


Tools need to be downloaded:-
Hcxdumptool
Hcxpcaptool
Hashcat

Steps:-
ü¶†1] Request PMKID from the router

Unlike older techniques where you had to wait until a user connected to the access point so that you can capture the¬†4-way handshake¬†that is of¬†EAPOL.This new method for finding out the password credentials does not require that anymore. The attack works on the RSN-IE or Robust Security Network Information Element. It only uses one frame which it requests from the wireless router.

ü¶†2] Install Hcxdumptool & Hcxpcaptool

This is a tool that will help you to capture the PMKID packet from the access point. After capturing the frame, it can also dump it into a file for you. Below are some features of Hcxdumptool:

Can easily capture identities and usernames from a WLAN.Can easily capture passwords, plain master keys, handshakes and PMKIDs from traffic on WLAN.

After installing this tool run the below command in the CLI.

$ ./hcxdumptool -o test.pcapng -i wlp39s0f3u4u5 ‚Äìenable_status

The command displayed above will dump the frame to a file.

ü¶†3] After doing the above step now you will need to extract some contents from the frame file. This will be in the pcapng format. You can easily convert this into a hash format which the popular program ‚ÄòHashcat‚Äò can accept. Use the below command to extract the pcapng file.

$ ./hcxpcaptool -z test.16800 test.pcapng

ü¶†4] Using Hashcat to Crack the Wifi Password (WPA PSK Pre-Shared Key Recovery)

Hashcat¬†is a tool used a lot in the security and penetration testing field. It is used by both hackers and researchers for finding out passwords by cracking their hash. After finding out the hash of the password you can enter the password in hashcat and it will find it out for you. It will take some time depending on how complex the password is of the wireless network. Enter the cmd below and run hashcat.

$ ./hashcat -m 16800 test.16800 -a 3 -w 3 ‚Äò?l?l?l?l?l?lt!‚Äô

You need some brain, basic knowledge and patience

D
DRAGON COVENANT 29.04.2019 14:51:10
In this post we are going to discuss about remaining attributes of <table> tag -

üëâ summary - it is used to define a summary of the content of the table. It has no visual effects so it will not display anything in any browser but can be used by Screen readers...

Syntax - <table summary="text">
_____________________________________
üëâcellpadding - It is used to define the space between cell wall and cell content.
We give the value of cellpadding in pixels...

Syntax - <table cellpadding="pixel">
For ex. - <table cellpadding="15">
_____________________________________
üëâcellspacing - It is used to define the space between cells. We give the value of cellspacing in pixels...

Syntax - <table cellspacing="pixel">
For ex. - <table cellspacing="15">
_____________________________________
üëârules - It is used to define which part of the inside border of a table will be visible.

Syntax - <table rules="value">

It contains different types of value which are as follows -

1. none - It is used to define that no inside border of a table should be visible.

Syntax - <table rules="none">

2. rows - It is used to define that only row borders inside the table should be visible.

Syntax - <table rules="rows">

3. cols - It is used to define that only column borders inside the table should be visible.

Syntax - <table rules="cols">

4. all - It is used to define that both row and column borders inside the table should be visible.

Syntax - <table rules="all">

5. groups - It is used to define that row and column group borders inside the table should be visible.

Syntax - <table rules="groups">
_____________________________________
I apologize from everyone for not posting anything from three days. I was busy One attribute is remaining of table we will discuss tomorrow..

Note :- These attributes are deprecated from html5. On request of everyone I am postingüôÇ

What is a directory? üî∑

A directory is called a directory of folders and files. We want to find the directories of a site to get the information we want
Work with the CrawlBox tool (scan the directory) üî∑

First, enter the command in your terminal to install the tool

Go to the downloaded folder

Install the tool prefix with the following command

To run the main file using Python, enter the following command

python crawlbox.py

To view the help, you can click the following command

python crawlbox.py

-h

python crawlbox.py site.com -w list.txt
